These results were consistent with the preliminary results released on July 14, 2015.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:6pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:6pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:6pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:6pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Second quarter constant dollar</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;below the prior year quarter. Including the impact of foreign currency, reported sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">7%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;below the prior year quarter.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; GAAP EPS was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$0.80</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">.</font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Full-year constant dollar sales growth is expected in the range of 0% to 2% above the prior year. Including the impact of foreign exchange, full-year reported sales performance is expected to be 2% to 4% below the prior year. </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;padding-left:24px;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;"><tr><td style="width:24px;"></td><td></td></tr><tr><td style="vertical-align:top"><div style="line-height:120%;font-size:12pt;padding-left:0px;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8226;</font></div></td><td style="vertical-align:top;"><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Full-year non-GAAP EPS is expected to be $3.63 to $3.78 and GAAP EPS is expected to be between $3.56 and $3.71. </font></div></td></tr></table><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:6pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:6pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:6pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:6pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#8220;We faced a number of challenges in the second quarter and that is reflected in our results,&#8221; said Kasper Jakobsen, Chief Executive Officer. &#8220;While we are pleased with our strong performance in North America and Europe, we are determined to improve performance in specific Asian and Latin American markets. While disappointed with our overall sales in China in the latest quarter, we are encouraged by the early trajectory of our new growth initiatives there - and expect to see a return to sequential quarterly growth within the year. We remain committed to investing in support of our long term strategy.&#8221;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter Company Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Constant dollar sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;lower than the prior year. Volume declines in Asia and Latin America were partially offset by improved pricing and performance in the U.S. business. Foreign exchange adversely impacted reported second quarter sales which were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$1,032.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$1,111.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the same quarter of the prior year.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Gross margin was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">65.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, up from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">61.6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2014 mainly due to lower dairy costs which benefited all segments. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><sup style="vertical-align:top;line-height:120%;font-size:8pt">(1)</sup></font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-style:italic;">&#32;Constant dollar figures exclude the impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates and non-GAAP results exclude Specified Items. For a description of Specified Items, and a reconciliation of non-GAAP to GAAP and constant dollar results, see the schedules titled &#8220;Supplemental Financial Information&#8221; and &#8220;Reconciliation of Non-GAAP to GAAP Results.&#8221;</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Page </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">1</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;of 12</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s92995A91B75B5BDF98FEC753C92F95D9"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Investment in advertising and promotion was 18.4% of sales, reflecting the company&#8217;s continued commitment to key growth initiatives, notably in China. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Earnings before interest and income taxes (&#8220;EBIT&#8221;) totaled </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$229.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2015 compared to the </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$244.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the prior year quarter. Despite higher gross margin, EBIT was below the prior year as a result of lower revenue and increased investment in demand creation.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">The company&#8217;s effective tax rate (&#8220;ETR&#8221;) was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">24.5%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the second quarter, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">23.3%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the prior year quarter. The higher ETR reflected a change in geographic earnings mix toward jurisdictions with higher tax rates.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Net earnings attributable to shareholders were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$162.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$171.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the prior year quarter.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-weight:bold;">Second Quarter Segment Results</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">North America/Europe</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">North America/Europe segment sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">6%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;higher than the prior year on a constant dollar basis. On a reported basis, sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$320.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, up from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$311.1 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the same period a year ago. Sales growth was mainly driven by improved pricing.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Gross margin in the segment improved compared to the prior year quarter. Despite strong investment in advertising and promotion, operating expenses in total were lower as a percentage of sales which resulted in an EBIT margin improvement of 470 basis points over the second quarter 2014 to 26.6%. Second quarter EBIT of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$85.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;was 25% higher than the prior year quarter of $68.0 million.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">Latin America</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Latin America segment sales increased </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">1%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;on a constant dollar basis. Pricing gains in the overall segment more than offset lower volume caused by competitor</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">s price-based promotional activity in the Mexican market and restricted shipments in Venezuela. Foreign exchange adversely affected reported sales of </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$198.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$224.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the same period a year ago.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Gross margin improved over the prior year quarter and helped fund additional investment in demand creation on a constant currency basis. Operating expenses were slightly higher than the comparative period due to the absence of a prior year one-time gain. EBIT was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$44.8 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$53.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the same quarter of 2014. </font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">Asia</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Constant dollar sales in the Asia segment were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">10%</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;below the prior year quarter. On a reported basis, sales were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$513.2 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">, compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$575.6 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the prior year quarter. Sales were impacted by competitors</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:11pt;">&#8217;</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">prevalent priced-based promotional activity in China and Thailand that resulted in weaker market shares within the period. In addition, Hong Kong sales remained at levels below last year&#8217;s average.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">EBIT was </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$156.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;compared to </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$195.9 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the same quarter a year ago. Higher gross margin  was more than offset by investments in demand-generating activities, mainly in support of new product introductions in China.</font></div><br><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:center;font-size:10pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">Page </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">2</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;">&#32;of 12</font></div></div><hr style="page-break-after:always"><a name="s92995A91B75B5BDF98FEC753C92F95D9"></a><div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:left;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div></div><br><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;font-style:italic;">Corporate and Other</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;"><br></font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">Corporate and Other expenses were </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$57.3 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;for the second quarter of 2015, down from </font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">$72.4 million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the second quarter of 2014 mainly due to current year actuarial gains that compared favorably to prior year actuarial losses related to a pension plan. million</font><font style="font-family:inherit;font-size:12pt;">&#32;in the prior year period.</font></div><div style="line-height:120%;text-align:justify;font-size:12pt;"><font
